--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_F-150/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_F-150/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_F-150/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_F-150/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)

local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_F-150/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

--[[

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart)

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local L1 = elsModule(ELSModel.L1);
	local L2 = elsModule(ELSModel.L2);
	local L3 = elsModule(ELSModel.L3);
	local L4 = elsModule(ELSModel.L4);
	local L5 = elsModule(ELSModel.L5);
	local L6 = elsModule(ELSModel.L6);
	local L7 = elsModule(ELSModel.L7);
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2);
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3);
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4);
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5);
	local F6 = elsModule(ELSModel.F6);
	local F7 = elsModule(ELSModel.F7);
	local M1 = elsModule(ELSModel.M1);
	local M2 = elsModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = elsModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = elsModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = elsModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = elsModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = elsModule(ELSModel.M7);
	local M8 = elsModule(ELSModel.M8);


	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					F1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));					
					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));				
					L1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					L2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					L3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					L4(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));				
					wait(0.07)

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(1);
					L3(0);
					L4(0);
					wait(0.07)

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(0);
					L3(0);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.07)					

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(0);
					L2(0);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.07)							

					F1(0);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(0);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.07)						

					F1(0);
					F2(0);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.07)							

					F1(1);
					F2(0);
					F3(0);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_F-150_Bedcap/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-150 Bedcap → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_F-150_Bedcap/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-150 Bedcap → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_F-150_Bedcap/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-150 Bedcap → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_F-150_Bedcap/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-150 Bedcap → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_F-150_Bedcap/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-150 Bedcap → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)

	--Front under lights
	local G1 = elsModule(ELSModel.G1)
	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.G2)
	local G3 = elsModule(ELSModel.G3)
	local G4 = elsModule(ELSModel.G4)
	local G5 = elsModule(ELSModel.G5)
	local G6 = elsModule(ELSModel.G6)

	--Front lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)

	--Back lights lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F2(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F3(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F4(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));					
					wait()						

				end
			end)
		end)()

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					G1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					G2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					G3(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					G4(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));	
					G5(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					G6(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));													
					wait()						
				end
			end)
		end)()				

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					R2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));														
					wait()						
				end
			end)
		end)()			



	else
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
		G1(1)
		G2(1)
		G3(1)
		G4(1)
		G5(1)
		G6(1)
	end
end

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)

	--Front under lights
	local G1 = elsModule(ELSModel.G1)
	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.G2)
	local G3 = elsModule(ELSModel.G3)
	local G4 = elsModule(ELSModel.G4)
	local G5 = elsModule(ELSModel.G5)
	local G6 = elsModule(ELSModel.G6)
	
	--Front lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)

	--Back lights lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
				F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0));
				F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0));
				F4(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));					
				wait(0.12)

				F4(1);					
				wait(0.09)

				F4(0);					
				wait(0.12)					
					
				F1(1);	
				F2(1);	
				F3(1);	
				F4(1);

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_F-350/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_F-350/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_F-350/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_F-350/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_G_Wagon/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC G Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;

	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC G Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		for _,v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		end
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for _,v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		end
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_G_Wagon/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC G Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;

					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.05)	

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.05)	

				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do	
					F5(0);
					F6(0);
					F7(0);
					L5(0);
					L6(0);
					L7(0);				
					wait(0.13)	
					
					F5(1);
					F6(1);
					F7(1);
					L5(1);
					L6(1);
					L7(1);				
					wait(0.08)	
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do	
					M1(1, Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0));
					M2(1, Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0));		
					M3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					M4(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));				
					M5(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					M6(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					M7(1, Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0));
					M8(1, Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0));			
					wait(0.07)
					
					M1(1);
					M2(1);	
					M3(0);
					M4(0);
					M5(0);
					M6(0);
					M7(1);
					M8(1);					
					wait(0.07)	

					M1(1);
					M2(0);	
					M3(0);
					M4(1);
					M5(1);
					M6(0);
					M7(0);
					M8(1);					
					wait(0.07)						

					M1(0);
					M2(0);	
					M3(1);
					M4(1);
					M5(1);
					M6(1);
					M7(0);
					M8(0);					
					wait(0.07)						

					M1(0);
					M2(1);	
					M3(1);
					M4(1);
					M5(1);
					M6(1);
					M7(1);
					M8(0);					
					wait(0.07)						

					M1(1);
					M2(1);	
					M3(1);
					M4(1);
					M5(1);
					M6(1);
					M7(1);
					M8(1);					
					wait(0.07)						
					
				end
			end)
		end)()

	else
		L1(1);
		L2(1);
		L3(1);
		L4(1);
		L5(1);
		L6(1);
		L7(1);
		F1(1);
		F2(1);
		F3(1);
		F4(1);
		F5(1);
		F6(1);
		F7(1);		
		M1(1);
		M2(1);
		M3(1);
		M4(1);
		M5(1);
		M6(1);
		M7(1);
		M8(1);
		M7(1);
		M8(1);		
	end
end


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Marked_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Marked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Marked_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Marked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Marked_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Marked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Marked_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Marked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1);
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2);
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3);
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4);
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5);
	local T6 = elsModule(ELSModel.T6);
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7);
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8);
	local T9 = elsModule(ELSModel.T9);
	local T10 = elsModule(ELSModel.T10);
	local S1 = elsModule(ELSModel.S1);
	local S2 = elsModule(ELSModel.S2);
	local S3 = elsModule(ELSModel.S3);
	local S4 = elsModule(ELSModel.S4);
	local Q1 = elsModule(ELSModel.Q1);
	local Q2 = elsModule(ELSModel.Q2);
	local Q3 = elsModule(ELSModel.Q3);
	local Q4 = elsModule(ELSModel.Q4);
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2);
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1);
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2);
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local W1 = elsModule(ELSModel.W1);
	local W2 = elsModule(ELSModel.W2);
	local W3 = elsModule(ELSModel.W3);
	local W4 = elsModule(ELSModel.W4);	

	if enabled then
		task.defer(function()
			while true do	
				T1(1)
				T2(1)
				T3(1)
				T4(1)
				T5(1)
				T6(1)				
				T7(1)
				T8(1)
				T9(1)
				T10(1)				
				wait(0.03)	
			end
		end)

		task.defer(function()
			while true do	
				F1(1)
				F2(1)
				wait(0.065)							
			end
		end)		
		task.defer(function()
			while true do				
				S1(0, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
				S2(0, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
				S3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				S4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				wait(0.12)

				S4(1)
				wait(0.135)					

				S1(0)
				S2(0)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.12)						

				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.135)					

				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(0)
				S4(0)
				wait(0.12)						

				S1(1)

				wait(0.135)

			end
		end)

				wait(0.065)

				Q4(1)
				wait(0.065)						

				Q1(1)
				Q2(1)
				Q3(0)
				Q4(0)
				wait(0.13)					

				Q1(1)
				Q2(1)
				Q3(1)
				Q4(1)
				wait(0.065)					
			end
		end)		

		task.defer(function()
			while true do	
				R1(1)
				R2(0)
				R3(1)
				R4(0)
				wait(0.12)	

				R1(1)

				wait(0.055)

				R1(1)

				wait(0.12)

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Sprinter/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights2;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = neonMaterial
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = smoothMaterial
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

	--Front under lights
	local G1 = elsModule(ELSModel.G1)
	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.G2)
	local G3 = elsModule(ELSModel.G3)
	local G4 = elsModule(ELSModel.G4)
	local G5 = elsModule(ELSModel.G5)
	local G6 = elsModule(ELSModel.G6)

	--Front lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)

	--Back lights lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F2(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F3(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F4(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));					
					wait()						

				end
			end)
		end)()

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					G1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					G2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					G3(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					G4(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));	
					G5(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					G6(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));													
					wait()						
				end
			end)
		end)()				

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					R2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));														
					wait()						
				end
			end)
		end)()			



	else
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
		G1(1)
		G2(1)
		G3(1)
		G4(1)
		G5(1)
		G6(1)
	end
end

	local G6 = elsModule(ELSModel.G6)
	
	--Front lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Supervisor_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Supervisor Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Supervisor_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Supervisor Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Supervisor_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Supervisor Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Supervisor_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Supervisor Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_17_Dodge_Durango/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC 17 Dodge Durango → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.BrakeLights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_17_Dodge_Durango/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC 17 Dodge Durango → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_17_Dodge_Durango/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC 17 Dodge Durango → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.BrakeLights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_17_Dodge_Durango/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC 17 Dodge Durango → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_17_Dodge_Durango/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC 17 Dodge Durango → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

		V2(1)
	end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_Explorer/PC_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC Explorer → PC Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_Explorer/PC_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC Explorer → PC Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_Explorer/PC_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC Explorer → PC Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_Explorer/PC_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC Explorer → PC Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_Explorer/PC_Explorer/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC Explorer → PC Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

					wait(0.035);
					K1(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					K2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.035);
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					V1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					V2(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					wait(0.06);
					V1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					V2(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					wait(0.06);
					V1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					V2(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					wait(0.35);
					V1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					V2(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					wait(0.06);
					V1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					V2(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					wait(0.06);
					V1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					V2(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					wait(0.35);
				end
			end)
		end)
	else
		B5(1)
		B6(1)
		B7(1)
		B8(1)
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
		B1(1)
		B2(1)
		B3(1)
		B4(1)
		F5(1)
		F6(1)
		F7(1)
		F8(1)
		K1(1)
		K2(1)
		V1(1)
		V2(1)
	end
end



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_Explorer/PC_Slicktop_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC Explorer → PC Slicktop Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_Explorer/PC_Slicktop_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC Explorer → PC Slicktop Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_Explorer/PC_Slicktop_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC Explorer → PC Slicktop Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_Explorer/PC_Slicktop_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC Explorer → PC Slicktop Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_Explorer/PC_Slicktop_Explorer/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC Explorer → PC Slicktop Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

	local B5 = elsModule(ELSModel.B5);

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_Bedcap_F-150/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC Bedcap F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_Bedcap_F-150/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC Bedcap F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_Bedcap_F-150/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC Bedcap F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_Bedcap_F-150/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC Bedcap F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_Bedcap_F-150/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC Bedcap F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_F-150/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_F-150/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_F-150/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_F-150/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_F-150/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_F-150/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:44
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_Slicktop_F-150/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC Slicktop F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_Slicktop_F-150/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC Slicktop F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_Slicktop_F-150/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC Slicktop F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_Slicktop_F-150/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC Slicktop F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_Slicktop_F-150/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC Slicktop F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Parks_Canada/PC_F-150/PC_Slicktop_F-150/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Parks Canada → PC F-150 → PC Slicktop F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:45
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)

	local A2 = elsModule(ELSModel.A2)

	local S2 = elsModule(ELSModel.S2)

					E3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					E4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					E5(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					E6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.09)						

					E1(1);
					E2(1);
					E3(1);
					E4(1);
					E5(1);
					E6(1);			
					wait(0.02)	

					E1(0);
					E2(1);
					E3(0);
					E4(0);
					E5(1);
					E6(0);			
					wait(0.09)	

					E1(1);
					E2(1);
					E3(1);
					E4(1);
					E5(1);
					E6(1);			
					wait(0.02)					

					E1(1);
					E2(0);
					E3(1);
					E4(1);
					E5(0);
					E6(1);			
					wait(0.09)	

					E1(1);
					E2(1);
					E3(1);
					E4(1);
					E5(1);
					E6(1);			
					wait(0.02)							

					E1(1);
					E2(0);
					E3(1);
					E4(1);
					E5(0);
					E6(1);			
					wait(0.09)	

					E1(1);
					E2(1);
					E3(1);
					E4(1);
					E5(1);
					E6(1);			
					wait(0.02)									
				end
			end)
		end)()					

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					Q1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					Q2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					Q3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					Q4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					Q5(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					Q6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					wait(0.09)						

					Q1(1);
					Q2(1);
					Q3(1);
					Q4(1);
					Q5(1);
					Q6(1);			
					wait(0.02)	

					Q1(1);
					Q2(0);
					Q3(1);
					Q4(1);
					Q5(0);
					Q6(1);			
					wait(0.09)	

					Q1(1);
					Q2(1);
					Q3(1);
					Q4(1);
					Q5(1);
					Q6(1);			
					wait(0.02)	

					Q1(0);
					Q2(1);
					Q3(0);
					Q4(0);
					Q5(1);
					Q6(0);			
					wait(0.09)	

					Q1(1);
					Q2(1);
					Q3(1);
					Q4(1);
					Q5(1);
					Q6(1);			
					wait(0.02)	

					Q1(0);
					Q2(1);
					Q3(0);
					Q4(0);
					Q5(1);
					Q6(0);			
					wait(0.09)	

					Q1(1);
					Q2(1);
					Q3(1);
					Q4(1);
					Q5(1);
					Q6(1);			
					wait(0.02)			
					
				end
			end)
		end)()		

	else
		T1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
		T5(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T6(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T7(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T8(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));						
		D1(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		D2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
		A1(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		A2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));		
		S1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		S2(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));	
		R1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		R2(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));		
		E1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		E2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		E3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		E4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
		E5(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		E6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		Q1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		Q2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		Q3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		Q4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

		Q6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));		
	end
